FROM (
    SELECT u."Id", u."FirstName", u."LastName", u."UserName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM "Follows" AS f
        WHERE u."Id" = f."FollowingId") AS c, (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM "Follows" AS f0
        WHERE u."Id" = f0."FollowerId") AS c0
    FROM "Users" AS u
    WHERE NOT (u."IsDeleted") AND u."Id" = @__userId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS u0
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT f3."Id", f3."Id0", f3."FollowingId"
    FROM (
        SELECT f1."FollowerId" AS "Id", f1."Id" AS "Id0", f1."FollowingId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY f1."FollowingId" ORDER BY f1."Id" DESC) AS row

    WHERE f5.row <= 10
) AS f6 ON u0."Id" = f6."FollowerId"

    WHERE NOT (f."IsDeleted") AND f."DeletedAt" IS NULL AND f."FollowerId" = @__userId_0 AND f."FollowingId" = u."Id") AS "IsFollowedByMe"
FROM "Users" AS u
WHERE NOT (u."IsDeleted") AND u."DeletedAt" IS NULL AND u."Id" <> @__userId_0
ORDER BY u."CreatedAt" DESC, u."Id" DESC
LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
